		var imageMapSrc = $('#image_map').prop('src');
		console.log('Image map orig: ' + imageMapSrc);

			imageMapSrc = imageMapSrc + '?ver=' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 5);

	<!-- /////// Backlog Map ////////// -->

	<div id="map">

	<div id="map-header">
		<div class="map-header-area"></div>
			<h1>How big is the backlog <span>where you live?</span></h1>
			<p>Though experts estimate that there are hundreds of thousands of untested kits in police and crime lab storage facilities throughout the country, there is no comprehensive, national data on the nature and scope of the rape kit backlog. Few state governments and no federal agencies track this data. Across cities and counties, there are vast differences in the way law enforcement officials track and report rape kit data, if at all, making it exceedingly difficult to compare data and to have a national picture of the backlog. <br /><strong>But here's what we do know.</strong></p>
	</div>

<div id="map-container">

		<div id="map-get-involved">
			<h1>what can I do to get involved?</h1>
			<ul id="involved-menu">
				<li class="involved learn"><a href="/take-action/learn-more">Learn <br /> More</a></li>
				<li class="involved action"><a href="/take-action">Take <br /> Action</a></li>
				<li class="involved effort"><a href="https://secure.joyfulheartfoundation.org/page/contribute/donate-to-end-the-backlog" target="_blank">Support <br />Our Efforts</a></li>
			</ul>
		<div class="clear"></div>

  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <h1 class="field-content"><a href="/blog/serial-predators-connection-between-domestic-violence-and-sexual-assault">Serial Predators: The Connection Between Domestic Violence and Sexual Assault</a></h1>  </div>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-body">        <div class="field-content"><p>Sexual assault, domestic violence, and child abuse are inextricably linked. While Joyful Hearts top policy priority is ending the backlog of untested rape kits, we frame this work to achieve our broader mission: ending this violence forever. This Domestic Violence Awareness Month, we explore the overlap between domestic violence and sexual assault, and how efforts to end the backlog have brought to light the prevalence of this overlap.</p>
</div>  </div>

  <div class="views-field views-field-body">        <div class="field-content"><p>The movement to end the untested rape kit backlog got a significant boost from the federal government this month when it issued the first-ever national guidelines for handling rape kits. </p>

  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <h1 class="field-content"><a href="/blog/portrait-serial-rapist">Portrait of a Serial Rapist</a></h1>  </div>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-body">        <div class="field-content"><p>Testing rape kits swiftly helps link crimes together and identify serial rapists sooner. Studies of perpetrators identified through testing backlogged kits show that serial offenders commit many types of violent crimes, including crimes against intimate partners and acquaintances.  James Drane of Detroit is one of the many perpetrators linked to both domestic violence and sexual assault. </p>
</div>  </div>

		<div class="action-homepage-wrapper wrapper">
			<h1>About END THE BACKLOG</h1>
				<div class="actionhome section_five">
				</div>
		<div class="clear"></div>

		</div>
		<div class="lower_columns">
			<div class="col_left">
				  <div class="region region-actionleft">
    <div class="column5 block block-block" >
		<h2>Our Purpose</h2>
	     <div style="float: left; width: 10%;">
<p><img src="/sites/default/files/icon-OurMission.jpg" width="22" height="20" /></p>
</div>
<div style="float: right; width: 90%;">
<p>END THE BACKLOG is an initiative of the <a href="http://www.joyfulheartfoundation.org" target="_blank">Joyful Heart Foundation</a> to shine a light on the backlog of untested rape kits throughout the United States. Our goal is to end this injustice by conducting groundbreaking research identifying the extent of the nations backlog and best practices for eliminating it, expanding the national dialogue on rape kit testing through increased public awareness, engaging communities and government agencies and officials, and advocating for comprehensive rape kit reform legislation and policies at the <a href="/ending-backlog-government-responses/local">local</a>, <a href="/ending-backlog-government-responses/state">state</a>, and <a href="/ending-backlog-government-responses/national-response">federal</a> levels. We urge you to <a href="/backlog/why-backlog-exists">learn more about the backlog</a>, <a href="/backlog/where-backlog-exists">where it exists</a>, and <a href="/backlog/why-testing-matters">why it matters</a>. We invite you to <a href="/take-action">take action and support efforts</a> to test rape kits. Help us <a href="/take-action/advocate">send the message</a> that we must take rape seriously.</p>
</div>
    <div class="clear"></div>
</div>
<div class="column5 block block-block" >
		<h2>The Latest Backlog Updates On Twitter</h2>
	     <a class="twitter-timeline" data-dnt="true" href="https://twitter.com/Endthebacklog" data-widget-id="392680408023703552" data-chrome="noheader nofooter noscrollbar noborders transparent" data-tweet-limit="5">Tweets by @Endthebacklog</a>

</div>
  </div>
			</div>

			<div class="col_right">
				  <div class="region region-actionright">
    <div class="column5 block block-block" >
		<h2>Take Action</h2>
	     <p><img src="/sites/default/files/advocate.jpg" width="26" height="25" style="float: left; margin: 10px 30px 45px 30px;" /></p>
<p class="inline"><strong>Advocate For Change</strong><br />You can help us end the backlog. <a href="/take-action">Advocate and help us spread the word</a>.</p>
<p class="inline"></p>
<p></p>
<p><img src="/sites/default/files/icon-support.jpg" width="25" height="25" style="float: left; margin: 30px 30px 35px 30px;" /></p>

  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <p class="field-content"><a href="/blog/creating-victim-notification-procedure-fayetteville">Creating A Victim Notification Procedure in Fayetteville</a></p>  </div>  
  <span class="views-field views-field-field-post-type">        <span class="field-content">Blog,</span>  </span>  
  <span class="views-field views-field-created">        <em class="field-content">November 17, 2017</em>  </span>  </div>
  <div class="views-row views-row-5 views-row-odd views-row-last">
      
  <div class="views-field views-field-field-post-type-1 Blog">        <div class="field-content">Blog</div>  </div>  
  <div class="views-field views-field-title">        <p class="field-content"><a href="/blog/supporting-cold-case-victims-through-notification-cuyahoga-county">Supporting Cold Case Victims through Notification in Cuyahoga County</a></p>  </div>  
  <span class="views-field views-field-field-post-type">        <span class="field-content">Blog,</span>  </span>  
  <span class="views-field views-field-created">        <em class="field-content">November 16, 2017</em>  </span>  </div>
    </div>
  
  
  
  
  
  
</div>    <div class="clear"></div>
</div>
<div class="column5 block block-block" >
		<h2>Featured Information</h2>
	     <p><img src="/sites/default/files/icon-resources-3.jpg" width="25" height="25" style="float: left; margin: 10px 30px 30px 30px;" /><span class="inline">When tested, DNA is one of the most powerful tools we have to solve and prevent crime. Read more about it <a href="/beyond-backlog/dna-and-rape-kit-testing" class="inline">here</a>.</span></p>
<p></p>
<p><img src="/sites/default/files/icon-resources-2.jpg" width="25" height="25" style="float: left; margin: 10px 30px 85px 30px;" /><span class="inline">As communities have begun to test rape kits, the question has remained of how to re-engage survivors whose cases are often yearssometimes decadesold. Read more about </span><a href="/beyond-backlog/victim-notification" class="inline">victim notification</a><span class="inline">.</span></p>
<p></p>
<p><img src="/sites/default/files/icon-resources-3.jpg" width="25" height="25" style="float: left; margin: 10px 30px 30px 30px;" /><span class="inline">Every state has a codified set of legal rights for crime victims, often called a "victims bill of rights." Learn about these rights <a href="/beyond-backlog-survivors-rights/law-enforcement-accountability-and-legislation">here</a>.</span></p>
    <div class="clear"></div>
</div>
